Script - // === Xalvis Chat Logic (global-safe) ===
(function () {
  /** run() holds your existing code */
  const run = () => {

    const bubble = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble');
    const popup  = document.getElementById('chatPopup');
    const msg    = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble-msg');
    const snd    = document.getElementById('bubbleSound');

    if (!bubble || !popup) return;      // basic safety

    /* â”€â”€ 1. GLOBAL toggleChat â”€â”€ */
    window.toggleChat = () => {
      const isOpen = popup.classList.contains('open');
      popup.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);        // show / hide
      msg.style.display = isOpen ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (!isOpen) snd?.play();
    };

    bubble.addEventListener('click', window.toggleChat);

    /* â”€â”€ 2. Other helpers (inline HTML) â”€â”€ */
    const now = () =>
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

    window.handleKey = e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') sendMessage(); };

    window.quickAsk = txt => {
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display','none');
      document.getElementById('userInput').value = txt;
      sendMessage();
    };

    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const txt   = input.value.trim();
      if (!txt) return;

      const chat = document.getElementById('chat');
      chat.innerHTML +=
        <p class="user">ğŸ™‹â€â™‚ï¸ You: ${txt}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display','none');

      const id = 'load-' + Date.now();
      chat.innerHTML += <p class="bot" id="${id}">Xalvis is thinkingâ€¦</p>;
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;

      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/chat', {
          method : 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body   : JSON.stringify({
            question: txt,
            token   : 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'     //  ğŸ‘ˆ same value as API_TOKEN
          })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        document.getElementById(id).outerHTML =
          <p class="bot">Xalvis: ${data.answer}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
        document.getElementById('replySound')?.play();
      } catch {
        document.getElementById(id).innerText =
          'âš ï¸ Sorry, something went wrong.';
      }
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
    };

    /* â”€â”€ 3. Pop sound on first interaction only â”€â”€ */
    let soundPlayed = false;
    const playBubbleSoundOnce = () => {
      if (!soundPlayed) { snd?.play(); soundPlayed = true; }
    };
    ['click','scroll','mousemove','keydown'].forEach(ev =>
      window.addEventListener(ev, playBubbleSoundOnce, { once: true })
    );
  }; // â”€â”€ end run()

  // Run now if DOM is ready; otherwise wait for it
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run, { once: true });
  } else {
    run();
  }
})();


********
Loader
(function () {
  let started = false;

  function initXalvis() {
    if (started) return;
    started = true;

    // 1. Load CSS
    const css = document.createElement('link');
    css.rel = 'stylesheet';
    css.href = 'https://www.smoothietexts.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/xalvis-style.css';
    document.head.appendChild(css);

    // 2. Load Widget HTML
    fetch('https://www.smoothietexts.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/xalvis-widget.html')
      .then(res => res.text())
      .then(html => {
        const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
        wrapper.innerHTML = html;
        document.body.appendChild(wrapper);

        // 3. Wait for DOM readiness before injecting the script
        if (document.readyState === 'complete' || document.readyState === 'interactive') {
          injectScript();
        } else {
          window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', injectScript);
        }
      })
      .catch(err => console.error("âŒ Xalvis widget load failed:", err));
  }

  function injectScript() {
    const script = document.createElement('script');
    script.src = 'https://www.smoothietexts.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/06/xalvis-script.js';
    script.defer = false; // â— Important: run immediately after injection
    document.body.appendChild(script);
  }

  // Lazy-load only on user interaction
  ['mouseover', 'touchstart'].forEach(evt =>
    window.addEventListener(evt, initXalvis, { once: true })
  );
})();

Chatot_api.py
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
#  chatbot_api.py â€“ Xalvis backend (STRICT KB logic + token + Supabase logging)
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
import os, ast, re, time, traceback, collections
from typing import List, Tuple
import datetime                                   # â† NEW (for readable timestamp)

import numpy as np
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request, HTTPException
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from supabase import create_client
from openai import OpenAI                          # SDK v1
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

# 1. ENV & CLIENTS â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
load_dotenv()

OPENAI_API_KEY = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
SUPABASE_URL   = os.getenv("SUPABASE_URL")
SUPABASE_KEY   = os.getenv("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")
TABLE_NAME     = os.getenv("SUPABASE_TABLE_NAME") or "smoothietexts_ai"
API_TOKEN      = os.getenv("API_TOKEN")            # ğŸ‘ˆ secure token

def _mask(s: str | None) -> str: return f"{s[:4]}â€¦{s[-4:]}" if s else "âŒ NONE"
print("ğŸ”§ ENV â†’", "OPENAI", _mask(OPENAI_API_KEY),
      "| SUPABASE_URL", SUPABASE_URL or "âŒ",
      "| TABLE", TABLE_NAME,
      "| TOKEN", _mask(API_TOKEN))

if not (OPENAI_API_KEY and SUPABASE_URL and SUPABASE_KEY):
    raise RuntimeError("âŒ Critical env-vars missing â€“ aborting boot!")

openai_client = OpenAI(api_key=OPENAI_API_KEY)
supabase      = create_client(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY)

# 2. EMBEDDINGS / SIMILARITY â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def get_embedding(text: str) -> List[float]:
    emb = openai_client.embeddings.create(
        model="text-embedding-ada-002",
        input=[text]
    )
    return emb.data[0].embedding

def cosine(a: List[float], b: List[float]) -> float:
    a, b = np.array(a), np.array(b)
    return float(np.dot(a, b) / (np.linalg.norm(a) * np.linalg.norm(b)))

SIM_THRESHOLD = 0.60

def fetch_best_match(q: str) -> Tuple[str, float]:
    q_emb = get_embedding(q)
    rows  = supabase.table(TABLE_NAME).select("*").execute().data or []
    best, best_score = "", -1.0
    for r in rows:
        emb = ast.literal_eval(r["embedding"]) if isinstance(r["embedding"], str) else r["embedding"]
        score = cosine(q_emb, emb)
        if score > best_score:
            best, best_score = r["content"], score
    return best, best_score

# 3. GREETING DETECTOR â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
GREETING_RE = re.compile(
    r"\b(hi|hello|hey|howdy|good\s?(morning|afternoon|evening)|what'?s up)\b", re.I
)
def is_greeting(t: str) -> bool: return bool(GREETING_RE.search(t.strip()))

# 4. ULTRA-LIGHT RATE LIMIT â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
RATE_LIMIT, RATE_PERIOD = 30, 60     # 30 req / 60 s
_ip_hits: dict[str, collections.deque] = {}
def rate_limited(ip: str) -> bool:
    now, bucket = time.time(), _ip_hits.setdefault(ip, collections.deque())
    while bucket and now - bucket[0] > RATE_PERIOD: bucket.popleft()
    if len(bucket) >= RATE_LIMIT: return True
    bucket.append(now); return False

# 5. ANSWER PIPELINE â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def answer(user_q: str) -> str:
    ctx, score = fetch_best_match(user_q)
    if score >= SIM_THRESHOLD:
        prompt = (
            "You are Xalvis, the friendly AI agent for SmoothieTexts.\n"
            "Answer ONLY with the information in the Knowledge below.\n\n"
            f"Knowledge:\n{ctx}\n\nUser Question: {user_q}\nAnswer:"
        )
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[{"role":"user","content":prompt}]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    if is_greeting(user_q):
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[
                {"role":"system",
                 "content":"You are Xalvis, a warm, concise AI assistant for SmoothieTexts. Respond with a short friendly greeting."},
                {"role":"user","content":user_q}
            ]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    return ("I couldnâ€™t find that in my knowledge base. "
            "Please visit our support page for help: "
            "https://www.smoothietexts.com/contact-us/")

# 6. FASTAPI APP â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
app = FastAPI()
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["https://www.smoothietexts.com"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["POST","OPTIONS"],
    allow_headers=["Content-Type"],
)

@app.get("/")
def root(): return {"status":"Xalvis backend running"}

@app.options("/chat")
async def options_chat(): return JSONResponse(content={}, status_code=204)

@app.post("/chat")
async def chat(req: Request):
    payload = await req.json()

    # ğŸ”’ Token check
    if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
        raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

    client_ip = req.client.host or "unknown"
    if rate_limited(client_ip):
        raise HTTPException(429, "Too many requests â€“ slow down.")

    user_q = str(payload.get("question","")).strip()
    if not user_q:
        return {"answer":"Please type a question ğŸ™‚"}

    try:
        bot_answer = answer(user_q)

        # â”€â”€ NEW 4-LINE INSERT INTO chat_logs â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        supabase.table("chat_logs").insert({
            "question"   : user_q,
            "answer"     : bot_answer,
            "timestamp"  : datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),  # UTC ISO-string
            "ip_address" : client_ip
        }).execute()
        # -------------------------------------------------------------------

        return {"answer": bot_answer}

    except Exception:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /chat"); traceback.print_exc()
        return {"answer":"Sorry, something went wrong. Please try again later."}

(function () {
  /** run() holds your existing code */
  const run = () => {

    const bubble = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble');
    const popup  = document.getElementById('chatPopup');
    const msg    = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble-msg');
    const snd    = document.getElementById('bubbleSound');

    if (!bubble || !popup) return;      // basic safety

    /* â”€â”€ 1. GLOBAL toggleChat â”€â”€ */
    window.toggleChat = () => {
      const isOpen = popup.classList.contains('open');
      popup.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);        // show / hide
      msg.style.display = isOpen ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (!isOpen) snd?.play();
    };

    bubble.addEventListener('click', window.toggleChat);

    /* â”€â”€ 2. Other helpers (inline HTML) â”€â”€ */
    const now = () =>
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

    window.handleKey = e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') sendMessage(); };

    window.quickAsk = txt => {
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display','none');
      document.getElementById('userInput').value = txt;
      sendMessage();
    };

    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const txt   = input.value.trim();
      if (!txt) return;

      const chat = document.getElementById('chat');
      chat.innerHTML +=
        <p class="user">ğŸ™‹â€â™‚ï¸ You: ${txt}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display','none');

      const id = 'load-' + Date.now();
      chat.innerHTML += <p class="bot" id="${id}">Xalvis is thinkingâ€¦</p>;
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;

      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/chat', {
          method : 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body   : JSON.stringify({
            question: txt,
            token   : 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'     //  ğŸ‘ˆ same value as API_TOKEN
          })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        document.getElementById(id).outerHTML =
          <p class="bot">Xalvis: ${data.answer}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
        document.getElementById('replySound')?.play();
      } catch {
        document.getElementById(id).innerText =
          'âš ï¸ Sorry, something went wrong.';
      }
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
    };

    /* â”€â”€ 3. Pop sound on first interaction only â”€â”€ */
    let soundPlayed = false;
    const playBubbleSoundOnce = () => {
      if (!soundPlayed) { snd?.play(); soundPlayed = true; }
    };
    ['click','scroll','mousemove','keydown'].forEach(ev =>
      window.addEventListener(ev, playBubbleSoundOnce, { once: true })
    );
  }; // â”€â”€ end run()

  // Run now if DOM is ready; otherwise wait for it
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run, { once: true });
  } else {
    run();
  }
})();


ChatGPT said:
Perfect, Jack â€” Iâ€™ve carefully added the new JavaScript logic for the lead form into your existing script without touching any of your current code.

Hereâ€™s the full appended code, with the new part cleanly marked and explained:

âœ… âœ¨ Append This Inside the run() Function (at the bottom of your current run = () => { ... }) BEFORE the }; // â”€â”€ end run() line:
js
Copy
Edit
    /* â”€â”€ 4. Lead Form Handling â”€â”€ */
    window.submitLead = async () => {
      const name = document.getElementById("leadName").value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById("leadEmail").value.trim();
      const error = document.getElementById("leadError");

      if (!name || !email || !email.includes('@')) {
        error.innerText = "Please enter a valid name and email.";
        error.style.display = "block";
        return;
      }

      error.style.display = "none";

      // Store in localStorage for reuse
      localStorage.setItem("xalvis_name", name);
      localStorage.setItem("xalvis_email", email);

      // Save to Supabase (via /lead API)
      try {
        await fetch("https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/lead", {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify({ name, email })
        });
      } catch (err) {
        console.error("âŒ Failed to save lead:", err);
      }

      // Show chat, hide form
      document.getElementById("leadForm").style.display = "none";
      document.getElementById("chat").style.display = "block";
    };

    // If form was previously submitted, skip it
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      const email = localStorage.getItem("xalvis_email");
      if (email) {
        document.getElementById("leadForm").style.display = "none";
        document.getElementById("chat").style.display = "block";
      }
    });

    // Track full chat for summary logging
    let xalvisChatLog = [];

    const originalSendMessage = window.sendMessage;
    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const userMsg = input.value.trim();
      if (!userMsg) return;

      xalvisChatLog.push({ question: userMsg, answer: null });

      await originalSendMessage();

      const lastMsg = document.querySelectorAll('.bot:last-child');

            name,
            email,
            chat_log: xalvisChatLog
          })
        });
      } catch (err) {
        console.error("âŒ Failed to send chat summary:", err);
      }
    });

Here is our chatbot_api. py = # â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
#  chatbot_api.py â€“ Xalvis backend (STRICT KB logic + token + Supabase logging)
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
import os, ast, re, time, traceback, collections
from typing import List, Tuple
import datetime                                   # â† NEW (for readable timestamp)

import numpy as np
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request, HTTPException
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from supabase import create_client
from openai import OpenAI                          # SDK v1
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

# 1. ENV & CLIENTS â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
load_dotenv()

OPENAI_API_KEY = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
SUPABASE_URL   = os.getenv("SUPABASE_URL")
SUPABASE_KEY   = os.getenv("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")
TABLE_NAME     = os.getenv("SUPABASE_TABLE_NAME") or "smoothietexts_ai"
API_TOKEN      = os.getenv("API_TOKEN")            # ğŸ‘ˆ secure token

def _mask(s: str | None) -> str: return f"{s[:4]}â€¦{s[-4:]}" if s else "âŒ NONE"
print("ğŸ”§ ENV â†’", "OPENAI", _mask(OPENAI_API_KEY),
      "| SUPABASE_URL", SUPABASE_URL or "âŒ",
      "| TABLE", TABLE_NAME,
      "| TOKEN", _mask(API_TOKEN))

if not (OPENAI_API_KEY and SUPABASE_URL and SUPABASE_KEY):
    raise RuntimeError("âŒ Critical env-vars missing â€“ aborting boot!")

openai_client = OpenAI(api_key=OPENAI_API_KEY)
supabase      = create_client(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY)

# 2. EMBEDDINGS / SIMILARITY â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def get_embedding(text: str) -> List[float]:
    emb = openai_client.embeddings.create(
        model="text-embedding-ada-002",
        input=[text]
    )
    return emb.data[0].embedding

def cosine(a: List[float], b: List[float]) -> float:
    a, b = np.array(a), np.array(b)
    return float(np.dot(a, b) / (np.linalg.norm(a) * np.linalg.norm(b)))

SIM_THRESHOLD = 0.60

def fetch_best_match(q: str) -> Tuple[str, float]:
    q_emb = get_embedding(q)
    rows  = supabase.table(TABLE_NAME).select("*").execute().data or []
    best, best_score = "", -1.0
    for r in rows:
        emb = ast.literal_eval(r["embedding"]) if isinstance(r["embedding"], str) else r["embedding"]
        score = cosine(q_emb, emb)
        if score > best_score:
            best, best_score = r["content"], score
    return best, best_score

# 3. GREETING DETECTOR â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
GREETING_RE = re.compile(
    r"\b(hi|hello|hey|howdy|good\s?(morning|afternoon|evening)|what'?s up)\b", re.I
)
def is_greeting(t: str) -> bool: return bool(GREETING_RE.search(t.strip()))

# 4. ULTRA-LIGHT RATE LIMIT â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
RATE_LIMIT, RATE_PERIOD = 30, 60     # 30 req / 60 s
_ip_hits: dict[str, collections.deque] = {}
def rate_limited(ip: str) -> bool:
    now, bucket = time.time(), _ip_hits.setdefault(ip, collections.deque())
    while bucket and now - bucket[0] > RATE_PERIOD: bucket.popleft()
    if len(bucket) >= RATE_LIMIT: return True
    bucket.append(now); return False

# 5. ANSWER PIPELINE â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def answer(user_q: str) -> str:
    ctx, score = fetch_best_match(user_q)
    if score >= SIM_THRESHOLD:
        prompt = (
            "You are Xalvis, the friendly AI agent for SmoothieTexts.\n"
            "Answer ONLY with the information in the Knowledge below.\n\n"
            f"Knowledge:\n{ctx}\n\nUser Question: {user_q}\nAnswer:"
        )
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[{"role":"user","content":prompt}]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    if is_greeting(user_q):
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[
                {"role":"system",
                 "content":"You are Xalvis, a warm, concise AI assistant for SmoothieTexts. Respond with a short friendly greeting."},
                {"role":"user","content":user_q}
            ]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    return ("I couldnâ€™t find that in my knowledge base. "
            "Please visit our support page for help: "
            "https://www.smoothietexts.com/contact-us/")

# 6. FASTAPI APP â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
app = FastAPI()
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["https://www.smoothietexts.com"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["POST","OPTIONS"],
    allow_headers=["Content-Type"],
)

@app.get("/")
def root(): return {"status":"Xalvis backend running"}

@app.options("/chat")
async def options_chat(): return JSONResponse(content={}, status_code=204)

@app.post("/chat")
async def chat(req: Request):
    payload = await req.json()

    # ğŸ”’ Token check
    if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
        raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

    client_ip = req.client.host or "unknown"
    if rate_limited(client_ip):
        raise HTTPException(429, "Too many requests â€“ slow down.")

    user_q = str(payload.get("question","")).strip()
    if not user_q:
        return {"answer":"Please type a question ğŸ™‚"}

    try:
        bot_answer = answer(user_q)

        # â”€â”€ NEW 4-LINE INSERT INTO chat_logs â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        supabase.table("chat_logs").insert({
            "question"   : user_q,
            "answer"     : bot_answer,
            "timestamp"  : datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),  # UTC ISO-string
            "ip_address" : client_ip
        }).execute()
        # -------------------------------------------------------------------

        return {"answer": bot_answer}

    except Exception:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /chat"); traceback.print_exc()
        return {"answer":"Sorry, something went wrong. Please try again later."}

âŒ Do NOT remove the id field. Keep it.

âœ… Why Keep id in Supabase
Reason	Benefit
Auto-generated Primary Key	Each row needs a unique ID for indexing and performance.
Better for Relationships	If you ever connect this table to others, id is ideal for linking.
Doesnâ€™t Rely on Email	What if someone types the wrong email? id avoids that problem.
Supabase best practice	Supabase expects every table to have a primary key field like id.

âœ… Recommended Setup
Keep id (type: uuid or int, primary key, auto-generated)

Set email as unique constraint, not primary key

Fast and stable indexing

Unique user identification

(function () {
  /** run() holds your existing code */
  const run = () => {

    const bubble = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble');
    const popup  = document.getElementById('chatPopup');
    const msg    = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble-msg');
    const snd    = document.getElementById('bubbleSound');

    if (!bubble || !popup) return;      // basic safety

    /* â”€â”€ 1. GLOBAL toggleChat â”€â”€ */
    window.toggleChat = () => {
      const isOpen = popup.classList.contains('open');
      popup.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);        // show / hide
      msg.style.display = isOpen ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (!isOpen) snd?.play();
    };

    bubble.addEventListener('click', window.toggleChat);

    /* â”€â”€ 2. Other helpers (inline HTML) â”€â”€ */
    const now = () =>
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

    window.handleKey = e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') sendMessage(); };

    window.quickAsk = txt => {
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display','none');
      document.getElementById('userInput').value = txt;
      sendMessage();
    };

    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const txt   = input.value.trim();
      if (!txt) return;

      const chat = document.getElementById('chat');
      chat.innerHTML +=
        <p class="user">ğŸ™‹â€â™‚ï¸ You: ${txt}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display','none');

      const id = 'load-' + Date.now();
      chat.innerHTML += <p class="bot" id="${id}">Xalvis is thinkingâ€¦</p>;
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;

      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/chat', {
          method : 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body   : JSON.stringify({
            question: txt,
            token   : 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'     //  ğŸ‘ˆ same value as API_TOKEN
          })
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        document.getElementById(id).outerHTML =
          <p class="bot">Xalvis: ${data.answer}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
        document.getElementById('replySound')?.play();
      } catch {
        document.getElementById(id).innerText =
          'âš ï¸ Sorry, something went wrong.';
      }
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
    };

    /* â”€â”€ 3. Pop sound on first interaction only â”€â”€ */
    let soundPlayed = false;
    const playBubbleSoundOnce = () => {
      if (!soundPlayed) { snd?.play(); soundPlayed = true; }
    };
    ['click','scroll','mousemove','keydown'].forEach(ev =>
      window.addEventListener(ev, playBubbleSoundOnce, { once: true })
    );
  }; // â”€â”€ end run()

  // Run now if DOM is ready; otherwise wait for it
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run, { once: true });
  } else {
    run();
  }
})();

// === Xalvis Chat Logic (global-safe) ===
(function () {
  const run = () => {
    const bubble = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble');
    const popup = document.getElementById('chatPopup');
    const msg = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble-msg');
    const snd = document.getElementById('bubbleSound');

    if (!bubble || !popup) return;

    // NEW: Chat log + user info
    let chatLog = [];
    let userName = '';
    let userEmail = '';
    let leadSubmitted = false;

    // === GLOBAL toggleChat ===
    window.toggleChat = () => {
      const isOpen = popup.classList.contains('open');
      popup.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);
      msg.style.display = isOpen ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (!isOpen) snd?.play();
    };

    bubble.addEventListener('click', window.toggleChat);

    // Helper: now() timestamp
    const now = () =>
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

    // Helper: handle enter key
    window.handleKey = e => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        if (!leadSubmitted) submitLead();
        else sendMessage();
      }
    };

    // QuickAsk shortcut
    window.quickAsk = txt => {
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');
      document.getElementById('userInput').value = txt;
      sendMessage();
    };

    // === NEW: submit name + email before chat starts ===
    window.submitLead = () => {
      const name = document.getElementById('leadName')?.value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById('leadEmail')?.value.trim();
      if (!name || !email) return alert('Please enter name and email to start.');

      userName = name;
      userEmail = email;
      leadSubmitted = true;

      // Hide lead form + show chatbox
      document.getElementById('leadForm')?.classList.add('hidden');
      document.getElementById('chatBox')?.classList.remove('hidden');
    };

    // === send message ===
    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const txt = input.value.trim();
      if (!txt) return;

      const chat = document.getElementById('chat');
      chat.innerHTML +=
        `<p class="user">ğŸ™‹â€â™‚ï¸ You: ${txt}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>`;
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');

      const id = 'load-' + Date.now();
      chat.innerHTML += `<p class="bot" id="${id}">Xalvis is thinkingâ€¦</p>`;
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;

      // Log user's message
      chatLog.push({ from: 'user', message: txt, time: now() });

      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/chat', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            question: txt,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        document.getElementById(id).outerHTML =
          `<p class="bot">Xalvis: ${data.answer}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>`;
        document.getElementById('replySound')?.play();

        // Log bot's reply
        chatLog.push({ from: 'xalvis', message: data.answer, time: now() });

      } catch {
        document.getElementById(id).innerText =
          'âš ï¸ Sorry, something went wrong.';
      }

      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
    };

    // === NEW: store full chat summary on exit ===
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
      if (leadSubmitted && chatLog.length > 0) {
        fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/summary', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            email: userEmail,
            name: userName,
            chat_log: chatLog,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        }).catch(() => {}); // silent fail
      }
    });

    // === First time bubble sound only ===
    let soundPlayed = false;
    const playBubbleSoundOnce = () => {
      if (!soundPlayed) {
        snd?.play();
        soundPlayed = true;
      }
    };
    ['click', 'scroll', 'mousemove', 'keydown'].forEach(ev =>
      window.addEventListener(ev, playBubbleSoundOnce, { once: true })
    );
  };

  // Wait for DOM
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run, { once: true });
  } else {
    run();
  }
})();

Here is chatbot_api.py code, add what you want y updating it in the full code itself and don't alter or make any other changes apart from this - # â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
#  chatbot_api.py â€“ Xalvis backend (STRICT KB logic + token + Supabase logging)
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
import os, ast, re, time, traceback, collections
from typing import List, Tuple
import datetime                                   # â† NEW (for readable timestamp)

import numpy as np
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request, HTTPException
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from supabase import create_client
from openai import OpenAI                          # SDK v1
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

# 1. ENV & CLIENTS â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
load_dotenv()

OPENAI_API_KEY = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
SUPABASE_URL   = os.getenv("SUPABASE_URL")
SUPABASE_KEY   = os.getenv("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")
TABLE_NAME     = os.getenv("SUPABASE_TABLE_NAME") or "smoothietexts_ai"
API_TOKEN      = os.getenv("API_TOKEN")            # ğŸ‘ˆ secure token

def _mask(s: str | None) -> str: return f"{s[:4]}â€¦{s[-4:]}" if s else "âŒ NONE"
print("ğŸ”§ ENV â†’", "OPENAI", _mask(OPENAI_API_KEY),
      "| SUPABASE_URL", SUPABASE_URL or "âŒ",
      "| TABLE", TABLE_NAME,
      "| TOKEN", _mask(API_TOKEN))

if not (OPENAI_API_KEY and SUPABASE_URL and SUPABASE_KEY):
    raise RuntimeError("âŒ Critical env-vars missing â€“ aborting boot!")

openai_client = OpenAI(api_key=OPENAI_API_KEY)
supabase      = create_client(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY)

# 2. EMBEDDINGS / SIMILARITY â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def get_embedding(text: str) -> List[float]:
    emb = openai_client.embeddings.create(
        model="text-embedding-ada-002",
        input=[text]
    )
    return emb.data[0].embedding

def cosine(a: List[float], b: List[float]) -> float:
    a, b = np.array(a), np.array(b)
    return float(np.dot(a, b) / (np.linalg.norm(a) * np.linalg.norm(b)))

SIM_THRESHOLD = 0.60

def fetch_best_match(q: str) -> Tuple[str, float]:
    q_emb = get_embedding(q)
    rows  = supabase.table(TABLE_NAME).select("*").execute().data or []
    best, best_score = "", -1.0
    for r in rows:
        emb = ast.literal_eval(r["embedding"]) if isinstance(r["embedding"], str) else r["embedding"]
        score = cosine(q_emb, emb)
        if score > best_score:
            best, best_score = r["content"], score
    return best, best_score

# 3. GREETING DETECTOR â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
GREETING_RE = re.compile(
    r"\b(hi|hello|hey|howdy|good\s?(morning|afternoon|evening)|what'?s up)\b", re.I
)
def is_greeting(t: str) -> bool: return bool(GREETING_RE.search(t.strip()))

# 4. ULTRA-LIGHT RATE LIMIT â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
RATE_LIMIT, RATE_PERIOD = 30, 60     # 30 req / 60 s
_ip_hits: dict[str, collections.deque] = {}
def rate_limited(ip: str) -> bool:
    now, bucket = time.time(), _ip_hits.setdefault(ip, collections.deque())
    while bucket and now - bucket[0] > RATE_PERIOD: bucket.popleft()
    if len(bucket) >= RATE_LIMIT: return True
    bucket.append(now); return False

# 5. ANSWER PIPELINE â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def answer(user_q: str) -> str:
    ctx, score = fetch_best_match(user_q)
    if score >= SIM_THRESHOLD:
        prompt = (
            "You are Xalvis, the friendly AI agent for SmoothieTexts.\n"
            "Answer ONLY with the information in the Knowledge below.\n\n"
            f"Knowledge:\n{ctx}\n\nUser Question: {user_q}\nAnswer:"
        )
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[{"role":"user","content":prompt}]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    if is_greeting(user_q):
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[
                {"role":"system",
                 "content":"You are Xalvis, a warm, concise AI assistant for SmoothieTexts. Respond with a short friendly greeting."},
                {"role":"user","content":user_q}
            ]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    return ("I couldnâ€™t find that in my knowledge base. "
            "Please visit our support page for help: "
            "https://www.smoothietexts.com/contact-us/")

# 6. FASTAPI APP â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
app = FastAPI()
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["https://www.smoothietexts.com"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["POST","OPTIONS"],
    allow_headers=["Content-Type"],
)

@app.get("/")
def root(): return {"status":"Xalvis backend running"}

@app.options("/chat")
async def options_chat(): return JSONResponse(content={}, status_code=204)

@app.post("/chat")
async def chat(req: Request):
    payload = await req.json()

    # ğŸ”’ Token check
    if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
        raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

    client_ip = req.client.host or "unknown"
    if rate_limited(client_ip):
        raise HTTPException(429, "Too many requests â€“ slow down.")

    user_q = str(payload.get("question","")).strip()
    if not user_q:
        return {"answer":"Please type a question ğŸ™‚"}

    try:
        bot_answer = answer(user_q)

        # â”€â”€ NEW 4-LINE INSERT INTO chat_logs â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
        supabase.table("chat_logs").insert({
            "question"   : user_q,
            "answer"     : bot_answer,
            "timestamp"  : datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),  # UTC ISO-string
            "ip_address" : client_ip
        }).execute()
        # -------------------------------------------------------------------

        return {"answer": bot_answer}

    except Exception:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /chat"); traceback.print_exc()
        return {"answer":"Sorry, something went wrong. Please try again later."}

# ... [your existing full code above remains unchanged] ...

@app.post("/summary")
async def save_chat_summary(req: Request):
    try:
        payload = await req.json()
        if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
            raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

        name      = payload.get("name", "").strip()
        email     = payload.get("email", "").strip()
        chat_log  = payload.get("chat_log", [])
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

        if not name or not email or not chat_log:
            raise HTTPException(400, "Missing required fields.")

        # Save full chat session to Supabase
        supabase.table("chat_logs").insert({
            "name"      : name,
            "email"     : email,
            "chat_log"  : chat_log,
            "timestamp" : timestamp
        }).execute()

        return {"status": "Chat summary saved."}

    except Exception as e:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /summary"); traceback.print_exc()
        return JSONResponse(status_code=500, content={"error": "Internal error"})

    if len(bucket) >= RATE_LIMIT: return True
    bucket.append(now); return False

# 5. ANSWER PIPELINE â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def answer(user_q: str) -> str:

    if score >= SIM_THRESHOLD:

            "You are Xalvis, the friendly AI agent for SmoothieTexts.\n"

    if is_greeting(user_q):

            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[

    return ("I couldnâ€™t find that in my knowledge base. "
            "Please visit our support page for help: "

# 6. FASTAPI APP â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€

    CORSMiddleware,

@app.get("/")
def root(): return {"status":"Xalvis backend running"}

@app.options("/chat")
async def options_chat(): return JSONResponse(content={}, status_code=204)

@app.post("/chat")
async def chat(req: Request):
    payload = await req.json()

    if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
        raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

    client_ip = req.client.host or "unknown"
    if rate_limited(client_ip):
        raise HTTPException(429, "Too many requests â€“ slow down.")

    user_q = str(payload.get("question","")).strip()
    if not user_q:
        return {"answer":"Please type a question ğŸ™‚"}

    try:
        bot_answer = answer(user_q)
        return {"answer": bot_answer}

    except Exception:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /chat"); traceback.print_exc()
        return {"answer":"Sorry, something went wrong. Please try again later."}

# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
# NEW: Chat summary endpoint to save { name, email, chat_log } to Supabase
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
@app.post("/summary")
async def save_chat_summary(req: Request):
    try:
        payload = await req.json()
        if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
            raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

        name      = payload.get("name", "").strip()
        email     = payload.get("email", "").strip()
        chat_log  = payload.get("chat_log", [])
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

        if not name or not email or not chat_log:
            raise HTTPException(400, "Missing required fields.")

        supabase.table("chat_logs").insert({
            "name"      : name,
            "email"     : email,
            "chat_log"  : chat_log,
            "timestamp" : timestamp
        }).execute()

        return {"status": "Chat summary saved."}

    except Exception as e:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /summary"); traceback.print_exc()
        return JSONResponse(status_code=500, content={"error": "Internal error"})
âœ… What to Do Next
Deploy this updated file to your current Render app.

Ensure your chat_logs table has:

name (text)

email (text)

chat_log (json)

timestamp (text)

No more individual Q&A logs â€” just clean session summaries!

Would you like a Supabase dashboard template to view these chats in a friendly UI?

  <!-- Script fix to control visibility and lead form logic -->
  <script>
    function toggleChat() {
      const popup = document.getElementById("chatPopup");
      popup.classList.toggle("open");
    }

    function submitLead() {
      const name = document.getElementById("leadName").value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById("leadEmail").value.trim();
      const errorEl = document.getElementById("leadError");

      if (!name || !email || !validateEmail(email)) {
        errorEl.textContent = "Please enter a valid name and email.";
        errorEl.style.display = "block";
        return;
      }

      errorEl.style.display = "none";

      // Hide lead form and show chat
      document.getElementById("leadForm").style.display = "none";
      document.getElementById("chat").style.display = "block";
      document.getElementById("chatInputSection").style.display = "flex";

      // Save lead data to global
      window.chatUser = {
        name: name,
        email: email
      };
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
      return /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email);
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>

You said:
Here is our script check, fix and rewrite the full code - // === Xalvis Chat Logic (global-safe) ===
(function () {
  const run = () => {
    const bubble = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble');
    const popup = document.getElementById('chatPopup');
    const msg = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble-msg');
    const snd = document.getElementById('bubbleSound');

    if (!bubble || !popup) return;

    // NEW: Chat log + user info
    let chatLog = [];
    let userName = '';
    let userEmail = '';
    let leadSubmitted = false;

    // === GLOBAL toggleChat ===
    window.toggleChat = () => {
      const isOpen = popup.classList.contains('open');
      popup.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);
      msg.style.display = isOpen ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (!isOpen) snd?.play();
    };

    bubble.addEventListener('click', window.toggleChat);

    // Helper: now() timestamp
    const now = () =>
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

    // Helper: handle enter key
    window.handleKey = e => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        if (!leadSubmitted) submitLead();
        else sendMessage();
      }
    };

    // QuickAsk shortcut
    window.quickAsk = txt => {
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');
      document.getElementById('userInput').value = txt;
      sendMessage();
    };

    // === NEW: submit name + email before chat starts ===
    window.submitLead = () => {
      const name = document.getElementById('leadName')?.value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById('leadEmail')?.value.trim();
      if (!name || !email) return alert('Please enter name and email to start.');

      userName = name;
      userEmail = email;
      leadSubmitted = true;

      // Hide lead form + show chatbox
      document.getElementById('leadForm')?.classList.add('hidden');
      document.getElementById('chatBox')?.classList.remove('hidden');
    };

    // === send message ===
    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const txt = input.value.trim();
      if (!txt) return;

      const chat = document.getElementById('chat');
      chat.innerHTML +=
        <p class="user">ğŸ™‹â€â™‚ï¸ You: ${txt}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');

      const id = 'load-' + Date.now();
      chat.innerHTML += <p class="bot" id="${id}">Xalvis is thinkingâ€¦</p>;
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;

      // Log user's message
      chatLog.push({ from: 'user', message: txt, time: now() });

      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/chat', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            question: txt,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        document.getElementById(id).outerHTML =
          <p class="bot">Xalvis: ${data.answer}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
        document.getElementById('replySound')?.play();

        // Log bot's reply
        chatLog.push({ from: 'xalvis', message: data.answer, time: now() });

      } catch {
        document.getElementById(id).innerText =
          'âš ï¸ Sorry, something went wrong.';
      }

      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
    };

    // === NEW: store full chat summary on exit ===
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
      if (leadSubmitted && chatLog.length > 0) {
        fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/summary', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            email: userEmail,
            name: userName,
            chat_log: chatLog,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        }).catch(() => {}); // silent fail
      }
    });

    // === First time bubble sound only ===
    let soundPlayed = false;
    const playBubbleSoundOnce = () => {
      if (!soundPlayed) {
        snd?.play();
        soundPlayed = true;
      }
    };
    ['click', 'scroll', 'mousemove', 'keydown'].forEach(ev =>
      window.addEventListener(ev, playBubbleSoundOnce, { once: true })
    );
  };

  // Wait for DOM
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run, { once: true });
  } else {
    run();
  }
})();

// === Xalvis Chat Logic (global-safe) ===
(function () {
  const run = () => {
    const bubble = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble');
    const popup = document.getElementById('chatPopup');
    const msg = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble-msg');
    const snd = document.getElementById('bubbleSound');

    if (!bubble || !popup) return;

    let chatLog = '';
    let userName = '';
    let userEmail = '';
    let leadSubmitted = false;

    // === Toggle popup ===
    window.toggleChat = () => {
      const isOpen = popup.classList.contains('open');
      popup.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);
      msg.style.display = isOpen ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (!isOpen) snd?.play();
    };

    bubble.addEventListener('click', window.toggleChat);

    // Helper: now() timestamp
    const now = () =>
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

    // Helper: handle Enter
    window.handleKey = e => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        if (!leadSubmitted) submitLead();
        else sendMessage();
      }
    };

    // QuickAsk shortcut
    window.quickAsk = txt => {
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');
      document.getElementById('userInput').value = txt;
      sendMessage();
    };

    // === Submit name + email before chat ===
    window.submitLead = () => {
      const name = document.getElementById('leadName')?.value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById('leadEmail')?.value.trim();
      if (!name || !email) return alert('Please enter name and email to start.');

      userName = name;
      userEmail = email;
      leadSubmitted = true;

      // Hide lead form and show chat box
      document.getElementById('leadForm')?.classList.add('hidden');
      document.getElementById('chatBox')?.classList.remove('hidden');
    };

    // === Send message ===
    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const txt = input.value.trim();
      if (!txt) return;

      const chat = document.getElementById('chat');
      chat.innerHTML +=
        `<p class="user">ğŸ™‹â€â™‚ï¸ You: ${txt}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>`;
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');

        const res = await fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/chat', {
          method: 'POST',

          body: JSON.stringify({
            question: txt,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        document.getElementById(id).outerHTML =
          `<p class="bot">Xalvis: ${data.answer}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>`;
        document.getElementById('replySound')?.play();

        chatLog += `Xalvis: ${data.answer}\n`;

      } catch {
        document.getElementById(id).innerText =
          'âš ï¸ Sorry, something went wrong.';

      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
    };

    // === Store chat summary on unload ===
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
      if (leadSubmitted && chatLog.trim()) {
        fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/summary', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            email: userEmail,
            name: userName,
            chat_log: chatLog,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        }).catch(() => { });
      }
    });

    // === First-time sound only ===
    let soundPlayed = false;
    const playBubbleSoundOnce = () => {
      if (!soundPlayed) {
        snd?.play();
        soundPlayed = true;
      }
    };
    ['click', 'scroll', 'mousemove', 'keydown'].forEach(ev =>
      window.addEventListener(ev, playBubbleSoundOnce, { once: true })
    );
  };

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run, { once: true });
  } else {
    run();
  }
})();

#  chatbot_api.py â€“ Xalvis backend (STRICT KB logic + token + Supabase logging)
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
import os, ast, re, time, traceback, collections
from typing import List, Tuple
import datetime

import numpy as np
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request, HTTPException
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from supabase import create_client
from openai import OpenAI

# 1. ENV & CLIENTS â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
load_dotenv()

OPENAI_API_KEY = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
SUPABASE_URL   = os.getenv("SUPABASE_URL")
SUPABASE_KEY   = os.getenv("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")
TABLE_NAME     = os.getenv("SUPABASE_TABLE_NAME") or "smoothietexts_ai"
API_TOKEN      = os.getenv("API_TOKEN")  # ğŸ‘ˆ secure token

def _mask(s: str | None) -> str: return f"{s[:4]}â€¦{s[-4:]}" if s else "âŒ NONE"
print("ğŸ”§ ENV â†’", "OPENAI", _mask(OPENAI_API_KEY),
      "| SUPABASE_URL", SUPABASE_URL or "âŒ",
      "| TABLE", TABLE_NAME,
      "| TOKEN", _mask(API_TOKEN))

if not (OPENAI_API_KEY and SUPABASE_URL and SUPABASE_KEY):
    raise RuntimeError("âŒ Critical env-vars missing â€“ aborting boot!")

openai_client = OpenAI(api_key=OPENAI_API_KEY)
supabase      = create_client(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY)

# 2. EMBEDDINGS / SIMILARITY â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def get_embedding(text: str) -> List[float]:
    emb = openai_client.embeddings.create(
        model="text-embedding-ada-002",
        input=[text]
    )
    return emb.data[0].embedding

def cosine(a: List[float], b: List[float]) -> float:
    a, b = np.array(a), np.array(b)
    return float(np.dot(a, b) / (np.linalg.norm(a) * np.linalg.norm(b)))

SIM_THRESHOLD = 0.60

def fetch_best_match(q: str) -> Tuple[str, float]:
    q_emb = get_embedding(q)
    rows  = supabase.table(TABLE_NAME).select("*").execute().data or []
    best, best_score = "", -1.0
    for r in rows:
        emb = ast.literal_eval(r["embedding"]) if isinstance(r["embedding"], str) else r["embedding"]
        score = cosine(q_emb, emb)
        if score > best_score:
            best, best_score = r["content"], score
    return best, best_score

# 3. GREETING DETECTOR â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
GREETING_RE = re.compile(
    r"\b(hi|hello|hey|howdy|good\s?(morning|afternoon|evening)|what'?s up)\b", re.I
)
def is_greeting(t: str) -> bool: return bool(GREETING_RE.search(t.strip()))

# 4. ULTRA-LIGHT RATE LIMIT â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
RATE_LIMIT, RATE_PERIOD = 30, 60     # 30 req / 60 s
_ip_hits: dict[str, collections.deque] = {}
def rate_limited(ip: str) -> bool:
    now, bucket = time.time(), _ip_hits.setdefault(ip, collections.deque())
    while bucket and now - bucket[0] > RATE_PERIOD: bucket.popleft()
    if len(bucket) >= RATE_LIMIT: return True
    bucket.append(now); return False

# 5. ANSWER PIPELINE â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
def answer(user_q: str) -> str:
    ctx, score = fetch_best_match(user_q)
    if score >= SIM_THRESHOLD:
        prompt = (
            "You are Xalvis, the friendly AI agent for SmoothieTexts.\n"
            "Answer ONLY with the information in the Knowledge below.\n\n"
            f"Knowledge:\n{ctx}\n\nUser Question: {user_q}\nAnswer:"
        )
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[{"role":"user","content":prompt}]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    if is_greeting(user_q):
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[
                {"role":"system",
                 "content":"You are Xalvis, a warm, concise AI assistant for SmoothieTexts. Respond with a short friendly greeting."},
                {"role":"user","content":user_q}
            ]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    return ("I couldnâ€™t find that in my knowledge base. "
            "Please visit our support page for help: "
            "https://www.smoothietexts.com/contact-us/")

# 6. FASTAPI APP â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
app = FastAPI()
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["https://www.smoothietexts.com"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["POST","OPTIONS"],
    allow_headers=["Content-Type"],
)

@app.get("/")
def root(): return {"status":"Xalvis backend running"}

@app.options("/chat")
async def options_chat(): return JSONResponse(content={}, status_code=204)

@app.post("/chat")
async def chat(req: Request):
    payload = await req.json()

    if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
        raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

    client_ip = req.client.host or "unknown"
    if rate_limited(client_ip):
        raise HTTPException(429, "Too many requests â€“ slow down.")

    user_q = str(payload.get("question","")).strip()
    if not user_q:
        return {"answer":"Please type a question ğŸ™‚"}

    try:
        bot_answer = answer(user_q)
        return {"answer": bot_answer}

    except Exception:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /chat"); traceback.print_exc()
        return {"answer":"Sorry, something went wrong. Please try again later."}

# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
# NEW: Chat summary endpoint to save { name, email, chat_log } to Supabase
# â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
@app.post("/summary")
async def save_chat_summary(req: Request):
    try:
        payload = await req.json()
        if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
            raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

        name      = payload.get("name", "").strip()
        email     = payload.get("email", "").strip()
        chat_log  = payload.get("chat_log", [])
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

        if not name or not email or not chat_log:
            raise HTTPException(400, "Missing required fields.")

        supabase.table("chat_logs").insert({
            "name"      : name,
            "email"     : email,
            "chat_log"  : chat_log,
            "timestamp" : timestamp
        }).execute()

        return {"status": "Chat summary saved."}

    except Exception as e:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /summary"); traceback.print_exc()
        return JSONResponse(status_code=500, content={"error": "Internal error"})

        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[{"role":"user","content":prompt}]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    if is_greeting(user_q):
        chat = openai_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-3.5-turbo",
            messages=[
                {"role":"system",
                 "content":"You are Xalvis, a warm, concise AI assistant for SmoothieTexts. Respond with a short friendly greeting."},
                {"role":"user","content":user_q}
            ]
        );  return chat.choices[0].message.content.strip()

    return ("I couldnâ€™t find that in my knowledge base. "
            "Please visit our support page for help: "
            "https://www.smoothietexts.com/contact-us/")

# 6. FASTAPI APP â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
app = FastAPI()
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["https://www.smoothietexts.com"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["POST", "OPTIONS"],
    allow_headers=["Content-Type"],
)

@app.get("/")
def root(): return {"status": "Xalvis backend running"}

@app.options("/chat")
async def options_chat(): return JSONResponse(content={}, status_code=204)

@app.post("/chat")
async def chat(req: Request):
    payload = await req.json()

    if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
        raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

    client_ip = req.client.host or "unknown"
    if rate_limited(client_ip):
        raise HTTPException(429, "Too many requests â€“ slow down.")

    user_q = str(payload.get("question", "")).strip()
    if not user_q:
        return {"answer": "Please type a question ğŸ™‚"}

    try:
        bot_answer = answer(user_q)
        return {"answer": bot_answer}

    except Exception:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /chat")
        traceback.print_exc()
        return {"answer": "Sorry, something went wrong. Please try again later."}

# 7. CHAT SUMMARY ENDPOINT â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
@app.post("/summary")
async def save_chat_summary(req: Request):
    try:
        payload = await req.json()
        if payload.get("token") != API_TOKEN:
            raise HTTPException(401, "Unauthorized â€“ bad token")

        name      = payload.get("name", "").strip()
        email     = payload.get("email", "").strip()
        chat_log  = payload.get("chat_log", [])
        timestamp = datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

        if not name or not email or not chat_log:
            raise HTTPException(400, "Missing required fields.")

        supabase.table("chat_logs").insert({
            "name"      : name,
            "email"     : email,
            "chat_log"  : chat_log,
            "timestamp" : timestamp
        }).execute()

        return {"status": "Chat summary saved."}

    except Exception:
        print("âŒ CRASH in /summary")
        traceback.print_exc()
        return JSONResponse(status_code=500, content={"error": "Internal error"})

function submitLead() {
  const name = document.getElementById('leadName').value.trim();
  const email = document.getElementById('leadEmail').value.trim();
  const error = document.getElementById('leadError');
  const startBtn = document.querySelector('#leadForm button');

  if (!name || !email) {
    error.innerText = "Please enter your name and email.";
    error.style.display = "block";
    return;
  }

  error.style.display = "none";
  startBtn.disabled = true;
  startBtn.innerHTML = "Starting Chat... â³";

  setTimeout(() => {
    // Hide form, show chat
    document.getElementById("leadForm").classList.add("hidden");
    document.getElementById("chatBox").classList.remove("hidden");

    // Add personalized welcome message
    const welcomeMsg = document.createElement("p");
    welcomeMsg.className = "bot";
    welcomeMsg.innerHTML = `ğŸ‘‹ Welcome aboard, <strong>${name}</strong>! Letâ€™s get started. <span class="timestamp">Now</span>`;
    document.getElementById("chat").appendChild(welcomeMsg);

    // Scroll to bottom
    const chatbox = document.getElementById("chat");
    chatbox.scrollTop = chatbox.scrollHeight;

    // Reset button
    startBtn.innerHTML = "Start Chat";
    startBtn.disabled = false;

    // Optional: play sound
    document.getElementById("replySound").play();

    // Save name/email globally if needed later
    window.leadUserName = name;
    window.leadUserEmail = email;

  }, 800);
}

You said:
Here our javascript please adjust it accordingly, full code, don't forget the starting chat you mentoned option as well - // === Xalvis Chat Logic (global-safe) ===
(function () {
  const run = () => {
    const bubble = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble');
    const popup = document.getElementById('chatPopup');
    const msg = document.getElementById('xalvis-bubble-msg');
    const snd = document.getElementById('bubbleSound');

    if (!bubble || !popup) return;

    let chatLog = '';
    let userName = '';
    let userEmail = '';
    let leadSubmitted = false;

    // === Toggle popup ===
    window.toggleChat = () => {
      const isOpen = popup.classList.contains('open');
      popup.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);
      msg.style.display = isOpen ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (!isOpen) snd?.play();
    };

    bubble.addEventListener('click', window.toggleChat);

    // Helper: now() timestamp
    const now = () =>
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

    // Helper: handle Enter
    window.handleKey = e => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        if (!leadSubmitted) submitLead();
        else sendMessage();
      }
    };

    // QuickAsk shortcut
    window.quickAsk = txt => {
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');
      document.getElementById('userInput').value = txt;
      sendMessage();
    };

    // === Submit name + email before chat ===
    window.submitLead = () => {
      const name = document.getElementById('leadName')?.value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById('leadEmail')?.value.trim();
      if (!name || !email) return alert('Please enter name and email to start.');

      userName = name;
      userEmail = email;
      leadSubmitted = true;

      // Hide lead form and show chat box
      document.getElementById('leadForm')?.classList.add('hidden');
      document.getElementById('chatBox')?.classList.remove('hidden');
    };

    // === Send message ===
    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const txt = input.value.trim();
      if (!txt) return;

      const chat = document.getElementById('chat');
      chat.innerHTML +=
        <p class="user">ğŸ™‹â€â™‚ï¸ You: ${txt}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');

      const id = 'load-' + Date.now();
      chat.innerHTML += <p class="bot" id="${id}">Xalvis is thinkingâ€¦</p>;
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;

      // Add to chat log
      chatLog += You: ${txt}\n;

      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/chat', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            question: txt,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        document.getElementById(id).outerHTML =
          <p class="bot">Xalvis: ${data.answer}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>;
        document.getElementById('replySound')?.play();

        chatLog += Xalvis: ${data.answer}\n;

      } catch {
        document.getElementById(id).innerText =
          'âš ï¸ Sorry, something went wrong.';
      }

      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
    };

    // === Store chat summary on unload ===
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
      if (leadSubmitted && chatLog.trim()) {
        fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/summary', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            email: userEmail,
            name: userName,
            chat_log: chatLog,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        }).catch(() => { });
      }
    });

    // === First-time sound only ===
    let soundPlayed = false;
    const playBubbleSoundOnce = () => {
      if (!soundPlayed) {
        snd?.play();
        soundPlayed = true;
      }
    };
    ['click', 'scroll', 'mousemove', 'keydown'].forEach(ev =>
      window.addEventListener(ev, playBubbleSoundOnce, { once: true })
    );
  };

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run, { once: true });
  } else {
    run();
  }
})();

(function () {

âœ… Here's What Went Wrong:

window.submitLead = () => {
  const name = document.getElementById('leadName')?.value.trim();
  const email = document.getElementById('leadEmail')?.value.trim();
  const errorBox = document.getElementById('leadError');
  const startBtn = document.querySelector('#leadForm button');

  if (!name || !email) {
    errorBox.textContent = 'Please enter both name and email to start.';
    errorBox.style.display = 'block';
    return;
  }

  errorBox.style.display = 'none';
  startBtn.innerText = 'Starting Chatâ€¦ â³';
  startBtn.disabled = true;

  // Delay the form transition to allow visual update
  setTimeout(() => {
    userName = name;
    userEmail = email;
    leadSubmitted = true;

    // Hide lead form and show chat box
    document.getElementById('leadForm')?.classList.add('hidden');
    const chatBox = document.getElementById('chatBox');
    chatBox?.classList.remove('hidden');

    // Replace welcome message

    chat.innerHTML = `

        <button onclick="quickAsk('How do I order?')">How do I order?</button>
        <button onclick="quickAsk('How do I signup?')">How do I signup?</button>
        <button onclick="quickAsk('Why do you need my card?')">Why do you need my card?</button>
      </div>
    `;
  }, 300); // Let the button update before swapping forms
};

(function () {

      const isOpen = popup.classList.contains('open');
      popup.classList.toggle('open', !isOpen);
      msg.style.display = isOpen ? 'block' : 'none';
      if (!isOpen) snd?.play();
    };

    bubble.addEventListener('click', window.toggleChat);

    const now = () =>
      new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

    // Helper: handle Enter

      if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        if (!leadSubmitted) submitLead();
        else sendMessage();
      }
    };

    // QuickAsk shortcut
    window.quickAsk = txt => {
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');
      document.getElementById('userInput').value = txt;
      sendMessage();
    };

    // === Submit name + email before chat ===
    window.submitLead = () => {
      const name = document.getElementById('leadName')?.value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById('leadEmail')?.value.trim();
      const errorBox = document.getElementById('leadError');
      const startBtn = document.querySelector('#leadForm button');

      if (!name || !email) {
        errorBox.textContent = 'Please enter both name and email to start.';
        errorBox.style.display = 'block';
        return;
      }

      errorBox.style.display = 'none';
      startBtn.innerText = 'Starting Chatâ€¦ â³';
      startBtn.disabled = true;

      // Delay form hiding to allow visual feedback

        userName = name;
        userEmail = email;
        leadSubmitted = true;

        // Hide lead form and show chat box
        document.getElementById('leadForm')?.classList.add('hidden');
        const chatBox = document.getElementById('chatBox');
        chatBox?.classList.remove('hidden');

        // Replace default message with personalized greeting

        chat.innerHTML = `

            Hi <strong>${userName}</strong>! Iâ€™m <strong>Xalvis</strong>. How can I help you today?

            <button onclick="quickAsk('How do I order?')">How do I order?</button>
            <button onclick="quickAsk('How do I signup?')">How do I signup?</button>
            <button onclick="quickAsk('Why do you need my card?')">Why do you need my card?</button>
          </div>
        `;
      }, 300); // Let the UI update before hiding
    };

    // === Send message ===
    window.sendMessage = async () => {
      const input = document.getElementById('userInput');
      const txt = input.value.trim();
      if (!txt) return;

      const chat = document.getElementById('chat');
      chat.innerHTML +=
        `<p class="user">ğŸ™‹â€â™‚ï¸ You: ${txt}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>`;
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('quickOpts')?.style.setProperty('display', 'none');

      const id = 'load-' + Date.now();
      chat.innerHTML += `<p class="bot" id="${id}">Xalvis is thinkingâ€¦</p>`;
      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;

      // Add to chat log
      chatLog += `You: ${txt}\n`;

      try {
        const res = await fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/chat', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            question: txt,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        });
        const data = await res.json();

        document.getElementById(id).outerHTML =
          `<p class="bot">Xalvis: ${data.answer}<span class="timestamp">${now()}</span></p>`;
        document.getElementById('replySound')?.play();

        chatLog += `Xalvis: ${data.answer}\n`;

      } catch {
        document.getElementById(id).innerText =
          'âš ï¸ Sorry, something went wrong.';
      }

      chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
    };

    // === Store chat summary on unload ===
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
      if (leadSubmitted && chatLog.trim()) {
        fetch('https://smoothietexts-ai-agent.onrender.com/summary', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            email: userEmail,
            name: userName,
            chat_log: chatLog,
            token: 'SMOOTHIETEXTS-2025'
          })
        }).catch(() => { });

    });

    // === First-time sound only ===
    let soundPlayed = false;

      if (!soundPlayed) {
        snd?.play();
        soundPlayed = true;
      }
    };
    ['click', 'scroll', 'mousemove', 'keydown'].forEach(ev =>
      window.addEventListener(ev, playBubbleSoundOnce, { once: true })
    );
  };

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run, { once: true });
  } else {
    run();
  }
})();

ChatGPT said:
